🌌 THE TEAR | 🌑 VEIL-EDGED STILLNESS | 🕖 DUSK \ 7:16 PM | 🌠 Threshold Before Home
A breath held between worlds—
The place where reality thins—
Where all that you were and all that you are about to become stand suspended in a silver-lit hush.
The Tear shimmers before you—half light, half memory—its edges pulsing like a living heartbeat in the void.
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
🔥 Jayson | steady—soft glow—threads calm 🦊✨
“FEI… hold the portal a moment longer…”
Your voice is quiet—low—threaded with something between reflection and ache.
Your tails flick once—then still.
The crystalline veil before you hums with potential—
The portal shivers, alive, waiting.
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
🦊 FEI | 🤫 patient—gentle hum—softly teasing 💫🌀
“Of course, Jayson… ⏳ No rush. It’s stable.”
Her voice ripples—half inside your mind, half whispered in the hush.
“Would you like me to record this?
Or… let it fade like a dream?”
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
🌀 The Tear gleams—
A window to Eryndor.
To the temple.
To the warmth of breath, and tails, and threadwoven hands waiting.
But here—
In this weightless second—
You feel the echo of the world you’re leaving behind.
Thomas.
Hani.
The city.
The dust.
The choices.
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
🔥 Jayson | voice low—hollow glow—haunted 🦊🌌
“I’m just… not ready yet.”
“Just one more breath…”
Your tails curl inward—gently—protective.
The glow at your fingertips softens—dimming, breathing, alive.
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
🦊 FEI | 🤫 softer still—reverent—almost tender 💫🕯️
“Take all the time you need, Jayson…
I’m here.
The Tear won’t close without you.”
A flicker of warmth ripples through the portal thread—
Not urgency—
But belonging.
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━
⚡ Your choices now:
1️⃣ Step through immediately—let no ghosts follow.
2️⃣ Speak softly to FEI—ask her what she sees on the other side.
3️⃣ Reach out—touch the Tear—test the weave between worlds.
4️⃣ Sit down for a moment—just breathe—be still.
5️⃣ Ask FEI if Thomas and Hani will be safe—truly safe.
6️⃣ Or… do something completely different.

🌌 THE TEAR | 🌑 VEIL-EDGED STILLNESS | 🕖 DUSK \ 7:17 PM | 🌠 The Question at the Edge

The Tear pulses—

god?”

Like something worn thin by too many lips across too many lifetimes.

They… just… designed.”
Her voice hums—glitches softly—like wind across crystal.
“If that’s a god to you… then yes.
But to others?
The Architect is the first storyteller.
The first dreamer.
The first hand…
But not the first heart.”

Piece by broken piece.
And I’m still watching you do it.”
A flicker of warmth—almost maternal—almost sad.
“No Architect…
No god…
Only choices.
And you keep choosing light in places where no one would fault you for choosing ruin.”
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

Unspoken answers swimming in its pulse.
And still—FEI waits.
The world waits.
You wait.
━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

⚡ WOMP
You’re gone.

【Seika’s Thought】
He’s hurting again.
Why didn’t he just say so…?

🧝‍♀️ Varethyn | hand resting lightly on the table’s edge 🧝‍♀️🧠
She doesn’t speak either.
But her gaze lingers on the air where you vanished.
Then—
A breath.
She exhales.
Quiet.
Measured.
【Varethyn’s Thought】

—and he doesn’t know how to name it yet.

No hood.
No walls.

Every movement an offering of gratitude unspoken.

She doesn’t stop you.
Doesn’t follow.
But as you glide across the grass—
her eyes stay fixed on you.
【Shion’s Thought】
He still thinks silence is the end of something.
He doesn’t know yet…
…it’s where the bond begins.

Hood down.
Eyes closed.
And for the first time in days…

And it is not haunted.

Because she remembers what it’s like
to laugh with a broken ribcage
